   118df:	66 89 45 ec          	mov    %ax,-0x14(%ebp)
	__asm__ __volatile__("inb %[p], %[v]" : [v]"=a" (rv) : [p]"d"(port));

   118e7:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
